***нереальность.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льность</a> (29637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальный.html>нереа́льный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nereálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nereálʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нереальность.html>нереа́льностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>unreality</li>
<li>infeasibility, impracticability</li></ol>

***нержавеющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нержавеющий.html>нержаве́ющий</a> (30429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нержавеющий.html>нержаве́ющий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neržavéjuščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>non-rusting, non-corrosive, rustproof, corrosion-resistant

***неряха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a> (31251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ря́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snappy dresser</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerjáxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́х</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> messy, unkempt person
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теперь.html>тепе́рь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:идти.html>шла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:опять.html>опя́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́чером</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:попасться.html>попа́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лице</a> семикла́ссник <a href = vnd.unilang:костя.html>ко́стя</a> оре́шкин — нескла́день <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tepérʹ že, kogdá šlá oná opjátʹ véčerom, popálsja na úlice semiklássnik Kóstja Oréškin — neskládenʹ i <b>nerjáxa</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Now, as she was walking down the street again in the evening, she bumped into a seventh-grader, Kostya Oreshkin  — an awkward and <b>unkempt</b> boy.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лик.html>ли́ка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:волос.html>во́лосы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скручивать.html>скру́чивала</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:редька.html>ре́дькой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:макушка.html>маку́шке</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>ре́дька</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:всегда.html>всегда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сползать.html>сполза́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грызть.html>гры́зла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноготь.html>но́гти</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чулок.html>чулки́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:плохо.html>пло́хо</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:натянутый.html>натя́нутые</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:морщиться.html>мо́рщились</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гармоника.html>гармо́никой</a> из-под <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:длинный.html>дли́нной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бки</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Líka bylá jedvá li ne prósto <b>nerjáxa</b>, vólosy skrúčivala rédʹkoj na makúške, i to rédʹka vsegdá spolzála na bok; oná grýzla nógti, i čulkí u nejó, plóxo natjánutyje, mórščilisʹ garmónikoj iz-pod ne sovsém ješčó dlínnoj júbki.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Lika was perhaps just a <b>messy</b> woman, her hair was tied on top with a radish, and the radish always slanted sideways; she had a habit of biting nails and her stockings were worn loosely, crumpled like accordions under her skirt that was not long enough at all.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неряшливый.html>неря́шливый</a> (15873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряха.html>неря́ха</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nerjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slob</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ря́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjáxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dandy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, shortening of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ряжо́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjažóxa</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dandy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рядиться.html>ряди́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjadítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dress up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ряд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rjad</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">row</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неряшливый.html>неря́шливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nerjášlivyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неря́шливее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неря́шливей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>untidy, slovenly</li>
<li>careless, sloppy</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ря́ш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:выя.html>вы́й</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>неряшливее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-неряш-</b>; суффикс: <b>-лив</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несвойственный.html>несво́йственный</a></b>

***несение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a> (31240)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">нес-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nes-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nesénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>carrying out, performance, execution; fulfilment
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:обязанность.html>обя́занностей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesénije</b> objázannostej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">performance of duties</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:несение.html>несе́ние</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инской</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:служба.html>слу́жбы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nesénije</b> vóinskoj slúžby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">carrying out of the military service</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:несказанный.html>несказа́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neskazánnyj</span>)

<ol><li>ineffable, indescribable

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> very strong, exceptional, extraordinary
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чрезвычайный.html>чрезвыча́йный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">črezvyčájnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:нескладный.html>нескла́дный</a> (15020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">скла́дный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skládnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нескладный.html>нескла́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neskládnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ungainly, awkward, gawky, clumsy</li>
<li>absurd</li>
<li>incoherent, inarticulate <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">speech, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>inharmonious</li></ol>
